He completed a residency at University of Illinois Hospital & Health Sciences System and served in several medical facilities in USA. Dr. Narayan specialized in Neonatal-Perinatal Medicine. Dr. Athi was an active member and a strong supporter of GATS. He has historically also provided significant financial support for many GATS activities. He has already donated money for GCC few years back even though we were not ready! He was a passionate philanthropist. He has done many charitable activities through American Tamil Medical Association (ATMA) and very passionate about helping poor in India. He was instrumental in building the Pallavaram Children Medical Center, a hospital for poor children in Pallavaram, Chennai which is doing an excellent service Also he motivated many youngsters to get into medical profession and helped Pre-Med students from USA by creating opportunities to do health-care related projects in his hospital in Pallavaram, Chennai. Dr. Athi's is also the founding President of ATMA GA Chapter. He conducted the national ATMA meeting in Atlanta within couple of years after coming to Georgia, which showed his leadership in bringing Atlanta Tamil medical professionals together. Dr. Athi is survived by his two sons and their families and extended families in India. We convey our deepest condolences to all family members. Funeral arrangements are being made.
